ͧ̋̈́̑͌ͩ͆̓̎̄ͧ͛̓̒́ͦ̾ͮ͏̷̵̪̬͕͚̠̰r̴̢̲̝̯̳̼̙̰̫͍͇ͫͣͯ͒̑̿͋̈̑͒͛͗̔̓̅̓ͧ͗̃́͠e̵͕̞͔̗̹ͧ͗ͬ͋̂ͯ̐ͦ̄͌ͥͧ͗̔̀̕vͩͫ̽̂͗͊ͪͬ̓̀͐͑͗ͬ̃̏̋͌҉̧̭̮̠̗ë̵̸̵̵̢͉̠͔̫̟̬̳̤̝̙̈́̽ͪ̏ͨ̀r̵̢͇̰̝̜͍̰̠͚̥̫̠̪̊̽͒̐͐̋̆̀̚͜͞b́͂ͩ̉͂̋̊̿̏̔͏̝͔͙͈̣̳̯̙̭̬̘͙̕͝r͌̉ͦ̉̌ͫͤ̑̉͒̿ͦ̌̓ͨ͂̿҉̲͇̱̻͍͘ȃ̢̛̝̩̞̪͍̹̲̺̣̣̙̬̞͊͌̈̑͋̃̐͘͠t̶̹̻̪͔͉͕̱͛ͦ̀̈́̈́͛́̿̃͂̏̄̂ͦ͛́͝ȅ̡̼̮̬̤̰͍̜̺͉̘̮̹͕͚͌͋́̔̎͆ͪ̎̄ͯ͐͜͠s̛̠͉̻̥̞̳̥͉͇̦̖̠̣͉̫̯͈̻ͤͤ̀̄̏ͫ͛̾̈̔̊ͥ̾̄̔ͩ̎̓̀ ̸̛̪͇͚̼̥̗̳̂̌̂̉̀̾͆̾́̚͘aͫͫ̅͗͗̂̾͂͗̿̆̇͑ͨͧͤ͏̢̛̠̱̙̗͈͎̼̫̦̗̗͈̞͕̺̼͟c̡ͧ̋̽̋͒͐͂ͯ̐̆̊͑ͧ̃́҉̸̤̜͓̝̜̝͇r̵̓ͧ̍̄͛ͪ̽̊̔̔̀҉̟̠̼͍̻̰̣͇͍̹̦ơ̵̖̦͓̗̹̭̞̺̤̞͎͖̤̗̝̆̒͛̌͐̌ͣ͞ͅs̡̥͚̰̰̼͚͔̬̽ͦ̋̉ͯ̚͘̕͠ş̴̡̯̖̫̜͎̜͙̮̻̪̯͍̭̌͆̈͋̏ͯͤ͐͗́̚͡ ̡̱̜͇̗̥̝̼̻̟̗̖͇͈̮͕͕̫ͨ͒ͦ̉́͌ͦ̓̃̀ͨ̋̀̚͜͞͠e̡̒̏̂͋ͨ̐̔ͧͣ̿ͩͣ͝͏̝̝͓̗̹͈̗͉̼͍͇͕͝v̸̨̰͓̯̩̠͖͇̗̩̘͂͑̂ͣ̔ͪ͌͆̑̒̀̀è̸̛͎͔͖͔̻̗͐̑̈́ͤ͋ͫͯ̂̂r̛͓̻̱̠͖̱͓̝̝̎ͬ̒͊͜͝ͅy̷̯̳̖͕͎̜ͦ̏̑ͪͭͫ̀ͅ ̶̨̹̳̩̣͙̫̩̫ͬͩ̍ͨ̐̐ͨ̽f̌͒̄̔̊̀́̈͒҉̨̬̲̼͕̳̹͇͓͙̠͇̰͎͍͎͈̖ȑ̟͉͎̳͔̫͚͕̟̥̼̞̹̥̦̐̄ͥ̀̀ͅȁ̢̡̘͇͈̜̼̙̟͕̻̣̑̊̋ͭ͑ͤ̓͊́g̶̷̶̡̟̞̖͍͎͖͕̭̙͕͚̘ͧ̃ͥ̋͆ͪͯ̊ͩ͒͊ͪ̈́͢m̪͍͕̝̝̹̉̓ͦ̉ͫ̇̏̋͊ͥ̂̍͛ͦ́̀ȇ̷̮̻̭̗̞̼͖͈͙̞̎̓̑́͛̒̉̿̀̊͌̽ͭ̃͂̕ņ̵̛̭͔̹̲̣̦͈̬̪̜͍̫́̽̽͊̋ͯ̔ͩͮ̈́̿ͫ̅ͦͯͧ͠t̡̡̛̮̘̺͖̫̭̥̦̦̦̠̻̼͗̑ͥͩ̇ͧ͑ͨ̎̀͜ ̌͐͌̋̒ͩͬ͋҉̶̵͖̼͖͈y̶̼͙̠̫̖͇͍̪̥̝̰̼͍̯ͬ̌͆̌ͮ̋̄̀͠ọ̸̯̞͈̲̫̰̾̐̇̈́ͯͨ̒ͤ̈́̉́ͅu̢̗̮͎̼̼̓ͮ͐ͬ̾̀͢͡ ̴̶̡̭̜̳̥̙̰̹ͭͤ̅̃̋ͪ͒̾t̨̫̭̩͕̥̝͇̝̬ͦ͂̀̋̓͂̀̓ͫ͂̆̓́͠o̵̟̯͚̻͇̩͕̰͔̓ͫͪ̅̉ͪ̉̌̐̽̽l̢͉̲̳͇͉̮͖̺̦̞̝̘ͬ̿̽ͫͪ̈͊̕ḑ̷̴̰̲̦̫̝͈̌̔̔̆͋͆͒̑̈̏ͥ͘ ̶͓̝̠͙̜̣͈̫̥̱̫̭̜̭̓ͧ̃͑̽̈̄̾̿̊̊̇ͤ̽̑ͣ̓̀̕͞b̛͙̱͇̹͚̫͎̱͈͉͖͔̝͙̤͈̘̀̄ͮ̍ͥ͂ͨ̆̚͘͢ȯ̵̢͈̟̺͎͚͓̣̥̠̺̤͍̘͍͒̑̒͂ͯ̅ͮ̊̏̊͂́͞ų̨̛͓̪̳̞̫̜͙̉̍ͮ͒͌ͦ̍ͯͣ̂ͥ̆ͬ͊̓ͭ̐͗͛́͡n̨̢̮̬̫͔͍̱̦̙̲͓͈̪̺͇ͭ̋͛͂̃̌ͫ̑̋ͤ̕͟͡d̡̗͕͔̤̦̮̙̖̫͚͚͖̼͖̓̒ͦ͌̚͘͝͠ ̎̒ͥ͒͒̆҉͞҉̹̮̭̬̼̜̱̰̯͇͚̬̙͕y̨̲̹̭̣̜̬̬͖̯͉̬͆̂ͨͨͧ̾ͭ̍̈̕͘ǫͫ̿̐̎̉̍̍ͪ̒̐̽̂ͧ̚̚͞͏̸̩͈̫̯͕̥͙̲̟͔̰̙͇̘͚̱̰u̫̖̘͚̞͍̲̯͈̘͒̅ͦ̽̇ͩ͆̃̅͗͑̀̚͢͟ ̌̀̓͑̈͑̐̇͊̈́ͧ͗͒̚͏̡͔̭͎͚̤̙͚͍̹͓̬͖̹͈̫̹̤͍̹͝t̸̛̼̯͇͚̯̞̼̭͍̥̤̺̬̖̺̰̝̉̅̓̈̊̄̓̓͌͊̿ͭ̐̓̍̈́ͮ͝ǫ̷̣̠̼͔̤͖̟͖̟̗͈͎̻͕̭̙̬̣͔͊ͭ̈ͯ̔͂͑̓̾́͂ͫ͆͟ ̴̡̧͔̜͖͖̦̖̣̲̫̩̤̟̗͚̯͕͑́̅ͥ͌ͬ͊̓͑̚t̷̴̵̼͓͈̪̼̫̬̻͔̩̭̹͈̩̖͂̓͐̎̀̀h̴̯̯̻̰̟̍̆ͣ́̊ͩ̂̆͡͠iͩͮ̄̑̆̆̽͒́̉ͯͦ̀ͦͦ̓͏̝̪̞̞̹͖͎̻͕͔̗̩̻́ş̺̦̳̣̤̗͍̦̖͎̱̭̭̎̔ͣͧ͛͒͗̌ͩ̈́̔͆͡ ͐ͫ̆ͨͤ́̿̿͂̈̓̍͒ͬ̚͞҉̠̹̯́͝ͅv̸̢̪̰͚̞̯͙̯̻͈̤̺ͮ́ͩͪ̎̓ͭ̍̀̋̑̇̓̆̐̾̑́ͯ̕͟e̊̍ͬ̽ͨ̈ͣ̕҉̵̨̘̥̜͎̩̠͉̙ͅs̶͎̱̞̭̬̰̰̲̠̻͈̜̖͎͔̲̘̣̟̉ͩ͗͋̓̇̆ͪ̋͋ͬͥ͒͊̎̔͘͜͞s̨̧̹͕̦̜̠̻̜̃̒ͭ̈͒ͣ̔͂ͣ̌ͫ̍̃̅̃̅̉͘e̷̘͍͙̫̝͖̠͚̠̲̲̻̪͚̺̦̋̒̂̽̇̅́͞ͅļ̶̷̸͇͔͓͔͉̠̘͉̱͙̿̓̂̈́̊̈͆̍͂̾ͯ̿ͥ́.̷̢͙͕̰͚̭̹͇͓̼̩͈̆ͧ̂̀̾̋̾̃͒ͩ̕\n̵̞̬͚̘͍̰̺͕̠̏ͫͮ̎̈̃̊͞͠͞\n̶͓̦̬͇̟̯̼̳̳̭͙̠͈̣̤̦̬͉̔̓̑͋̀͌̅͌ͨ̀ͬ̊ͩ͛̈́̚͢͞Y̬̫̥͍͍̰̙̣̼̙̯̞͙̬̙̣̯̲͆̐͒̓̿ͩͬͦͥ̎ͣͭ͝ò̤̯̱͍͙̗̞̠̪̪̗͖̪͓̓ͨ̈̅ͦͩ̓ͪ̅̈́̈́ͨ̇͐̐ͨ͐͝͡ͅu̴̻͈͙͓̣̣̮͆ͨ̌̑̑͊̎̐ͨ͊̒̐̆̈ͮ͑ͧ͠ ̸̷͎͙̼̪͈̖̗̳̺͚̮͉̝̖̄̿ͮ̄ͦ͊̍̏̂̑̑͂͐̾̚̕͠w̧͍͍̙̫̻̭̥̮̦̗̺̭̘̱͎͗̿̒ͩͭͨ̊͌͌͗ͦ͟͝e̷̡͙͖̰̮̬̬̹̥̞͔̱̥̮͍̲̩͌̂͌͊̑ͫ̆̊̋͗ͥ̇̍̚̚ͅŕ̢̺̤̲̲̞͇̻̤̣͉̫̘̦̘ͫͧ͊͛ͣ̅̽̔͐͛̔͑̀́͟͜e̢̩͉̤͍͈͓͙͆ͣ͊͗̑ͫ͟ ̶̡̧̖͙̺̗̲͙̮͈̬̖̰͉͊̎ͮ̈́̈͐ͦ͌ͅa̡͎̫̘̤̗͔͍̰̥̤̤̤̾̏̈͐̌ͫ̓ͬͮ̈̈́̏̇̏͗ͤ́̚ͅ ͐ͣͫͯ͛ͯͯ͛ͧ͛͐͛̄͋̐ͪ̋ͣ͛҉̸̛͉̬̥̪̟͓̺́p̏̏̅͆͂͋ͧͥ̾͏̷̸̮̠̯͙̼͔̀r̢̦̗͇̩̲̩̗̟͕̰̬͎̗͇̤͒̽̾͋̑ͯ͗̉ͫ̽́ͥi̊̈̀̊͂̽ͣ̄́̚̕͠҉͙͉̣̳̳̼͇̮̺͍̘̳͚̠̘̺͢s̷̸̡̧͇͓̬̹̮͙̹̼̺̦̘̞͉̯̦̠͙͔̄̾́ͦͤͧͫ̑͒̿̋̔͊̽͋̊͐́ͅoͦ͆̆ͧ҉̵̴͕̪̹̻͜nͣͭ͒͗̌̆͐ͤ̋ͯͧ͂͏̨̣̯̰̫̺͈̺̯͓͓̩͖̦ͅe̶̷̫͎̻̫̠̳̩̭̼̠͉̣̳̼̪͕͕̗̣ͫ̀̃͜͡͝r̸̢̥̭̫̙͙̱̂ͤͬ̾ͭ̆̽ ̸̨̡̯̼̪̫͖̲̂̔̎̋̈́ͤ̿̓̏ͩ́̒w̩̤̹͔̻̭͓̭̺̫̦̣̟̙̯̗̞͐̎̓̋͆ͪ͂̊̽̿ͧ̉̋ͥ̑̆ͧͯͧ͠h̵̨̨̙̳̤͕̪͎̪̘͖̥̹͖̖̤̦̘̺̰ͨ͗ͪͩ̍̆̾͊̓̂̚͟o̡ͧͪ́ͧͬͬ͒͋ͥ̾ͤ͊̐ͪ́̚͏͙̝͔͓̦͉͍ ̬̞̹͖̫̫̫͔̰̠̜̘͎̯̼̲̣̗̺ͤ̏̓ͣ͠ẁ̶̨̢̢̙̝̲̤͉̗͎̻̺̦͖͖̝̭̃̋͂̅͌͋͘ͅa̐̾ͣ̅̄͊̏ͩ̃ͪ̀̾̿̀ͦ͛̽͡͠҉̨̨̼̼̘͉̦s͙͉͈̹̰̦̜̮̬̰̠̙̮̳̲ͯ̎͗̑̚͟ ̢̡͉̗̰̠̠̼̜̹͖̝̞̼͕̲͎̩̗̤ͭ̍͂̈́͌ͭͬͤ̂̈͞t̨̡͔̟̳̼̾͂̽͂̒̀̾̉̀̔ͥ͌̊̄ͩ͢͢a̡̠̼̼̲̜̤͔͔̪̖̲͔ͨ̏̋̆͘͜͟s̴̪͉̰̬̘͓͇̱͍̟͛̽ͣ̎̂̽̑̿ͭ̈ͣ͆͜͝͡ṭ̥͖̪̹̥̩̘̥̙̬̘͎̭̫̫̿̃́̃́ͪ͒̄̃ͬ͋͘̕͜ͅi̙̦̘̺͉͖̞̤̬̩̖͎̫͎͉̐ͥ̆̓̄̑̉͂ͧ͘ͅn̶̢̦̖͉̰̞͚̼̖͎̮̣ͭ̉͂͌̋̑͆̎͑̂ͬͬ͋͊ͭͧͩ͛̚͘͘ǵ͑́ͣ͌ͯͯͬ̓͡҉̬̣͕̜̭̖̫̱̗̱̣̹̱̝̩́ ̷̧̤̪̥̲̻̣̳̥ͯ̉̀́ͣ̑̓ͪ̚͡f̵̢̩̮͕̳̪̺͙̻͉̩͚͔͈͖͓͛ͤ́̏̏ͣ͂̓̍̀͞ṙ̠̫̪͇̋́̄̾͊͗ͤ̏ͭͨ̋̅ͨ̊̋̓ͮ̚̕̕e̐̌̈ͯ̌̀̈́̇ͦ̿ͦ͗̃͆͌̀͐͂͏̮͖̣̮̹̙͖̼͟e̸̷ͪͨͫ̎̊͂ͯͫͦͯ̀́҉̤̰̩̞͖͍͚̼͔͓d̔ͥ̆ͯ̄̀͛̅̿̌͆̓̐̾ͧ̚͏̶̴̵̩͙͎̪̞͖̰͉̦͖̪̠͡ͅo̶̴͕̰̝͓͉̹̩̟̟̟͂ͧͬ͐̚͢͞ͅm̩̠̤̯͉̣̜̺̬̩̥̰̟̠͚̗͓͉̎̿ͫ͒ͬ̒̾ͪ͗͆͑̈́ͩͪ̈͟ ̸̶̸̧̗̤̦̯͙̭̪̠̯͙̤̹̓̏ͥ͂ͣ͑̽̀f̺̗͈͎͇̄ͨ͒͆ͭ̊̂ͤͣ͐̃̋̉̕͢͜ǫ̶̹̞̫̮̥̱͙̯̣̰͇͈̘̲̯ͤ̌͑ͭ̄͂ͪ́̕͞ͅr̸̢̛͓̩̭̼̮͕̤̖̦̓ͭ̄ͥ̊̇̓̋̀ͧ͟͢ ̵̡̩̟͓͕̇̐̽ͫ̾̏̌͊͗̆͆̂̃̈͐͐ͮͦ̚t̍ͣͨ̊̈͐̔ͨ̆̂̾ͮ̏͝͏̧̟̟͓̬͉͖͍̱͔̗͉̟͙̙̞̬h̃̓ͫ̀̾̆̂͒̋͐̾͞҉̤̖̝̰̖̱̱͚e̫͓̝͚̻̩͔̳̦͚̩͔̹̻̰̽͒̎ͧ̓͛̌́͐̉̔̈́̑̃̾ͤ̐͛́ ̴͎̪̙͎̜̙͖͉͔̟̿͑̑̑̔ͫ͑̂̽͂͑̊͂̌̊͗̾͋̚̕f̡̏͗ͮ̆ͭ̓͐́͜҉̶͉̥̞̯̦į̅͌͒̑ͨ͌ͬ͋̉ͥ͊ͫ҉͏̺͕̘̭̞͙͙͎͝r̶̦̙̱̹̫͉̹̥͖̱̤͂ͬͤ͆ͬ́̈́ͅsͦ͋̉ͫ͟͝͏̶͇̻̼̞̤̻̬̦̮̟͖͚̰̮̥͉̹tͩ̓͑ͣͣͯ̾̽̋̂̑̋̀̈ͥ̚͜͡҉̠͕̘̹͖̬̠͠ ̸̴̬̦̼͙̹͔͖̼̼̗̗̻̞͕̯̦́ͯ͊̉͊͊̾ͧͮͮ̃ͥ͐ͪͤ͘͠ṭ̵̶̨̥̦̪̩ͫ̓ͧͯͣ̈́ͫ͂̊̒͐ͬ͆ͫ̊̃̾ͣĭ̡̬̥̹̹̩̺͖͈̝̞ͭ̈̂͆ͣ̅̊̾ͮ̉͟͠m̡̯̖̤̟̼͉̔ͩ̌̚e͓̜̜̫̩̻ͬ̉̽ͬ͛ͣ̒̅́̚͝ ͕̰̻͖̞̥̼̼̫̖͒͐ͮ́ͮ̈̂̅̇ͬ̉͆ͥͮ̐ͩ͊͡i̶̧̹͓͓ͬͪ̚̚͢͠n̷̨̼̥̘̘̰̖͊̋̋ͩ̂́͘͠ͅ ̲̯̪̤͔͖̞̻̺͕̔̈́̀͆̓̇͑̅ͨ̉̑͋ͤ̓̐̋̋́̀ẗ̴̒̌ͦ́̕̕͏̪̻͙̰̳͙̳̙̗̝̦̖̙̺̪͎̦̬h̨͚̬̤͕̹̙̼̥̯̹̣̝͇̭͇̙̱͍̪̃̆̆̓̍̓̄ͫ͋̈̇͒͘e̒̔ͮ̈ͥ̍̊̽͞͝҉͉̮̰͎̮̬̫͖̝̗̬̩́ĩ̴̷͖̩̹̠̜͔̰͇͙͔̤̮̟̔́ͯͦ̎͆̔́ͯ̀̚͠r͔̲͎̮̫̼̫͉͓̪̪̜̭̝̻̖̠͑̂͑̽̕͠͝͞ͅ ̼̯̦̟̺̬̰͂̒̂ͯ̿̄̎́́ȩ̓ͫ̃ͥ̐̒͏̢̖̙̭̘͕̺͖̹͍̹̳̤̰x̴̜̣̟̦̪͚̭̹ͮ̊̋̆̋̋̄̾̿ͧ̐͟ỉ̍̑̀̄̀͟҉̤͕̥̭̼̖̪̳͈̬̯̦̻͉̫s̻͚̦̪̰̹͎̦̘̙͔̓ͭ͌̔ͮ͑ͯ̆̑̈́̾̊ͬ̕͡ť̷̪̼͖͔͈ͣͨ̄ͭͨ͗͜͟͝ę̵͇̲͎̗͉̗ͦ̌̐͛̓̽̃̽͐ͮ̎̏̍̂ͩ͌͂ͭ͌̀͞n̸͙̥̭͕̝̖̦̱̼̹̞͇̰͓̍̈́̾͗̃̈́̚͘̕͝c̨̮̯͍̫͈͌ͯ̽ͮͫͣ̋ͤͫͨ̆ͨe̷͓̞̠̻̖̱͓̫͍̭̖͇̺̮̲͇ͤ̄̌̀̅͛̓ͧ̕ͅ.̨̄͛͐͛̾͋ͯ̊͂ͧ̀̈́̃ͥ̈́̚͘̕҉̤͚͇̦̟̪̺̭̻̖̥\n̸̷̨͕̭̝͈͈̊̓ͬͨͣ͌̓̍ͮͩ́̚\n<div ̨͈̣̘̺̦͖̼̓ͤ̆̓́̑̉͒͋̑̾̀͌́b͙͇̪͇̹͖̭̬̦̋͌̋ͦ̀̚̕͡o̡̻̣͙̠̙̳̜̝͍̥̼̰̘͖̰ͩͭ̄ͮ́́ͧ̃̌̈ͨ̈̾͂ͫ̉̅́̚̕͜d̶̖̙̰̱̟͇̰̲̖̦͍͈͖̆̌̍̐̎̇͊̾ͣ̄ͨ̐̒ͥy̡͕͓̭̞̞͇͖̞̞͈̦̜̿̂̐͛̈́̂̃ͭͣ͑́ͬ̎͜͝͠ͅͅ.̊̌̍̔̎ͯ̾ͫ҉̸̶̴̶̻̬͍̥̬̫̙̹͕͙͕̪͖͎͕̠̞̞ ̡̙̘̥̟̙͓͚͖̮̹̱̣̪̻̈̉̓̅̈́͘͞ǫ̷͚͉͎͚̜̞͉̬̖̘̪̹̘̮̼̼̟͎ͫ͒̋̂ͫ̈́͒ͫ̑̈́͗̈͂͌̂̇ͤ̕̕n̪͓͕̠ͬͫ̓̑̎̂ͤͧ̋̔͐ͣ̀ͤ̀̚̚͢͡͡l̨̄͊̓̎ͪ̔̓̆̊̓̅͗̂̿͛̍̐͠͏̦̮͇̬͙ͅy̡̰̬͕̘̘̳̬̮̬̲̦̭̖͍̼̾ͬ͆̀ͮ̌̊̋́̏̎̚̚̕͟ͅ ̸̡̭̞̳̜͇̲͔͖͆ͥͩ̍ͨ̇̆̈́ͣ̈́̈́̀̔ͪ̅͑y̴̨̟̩̪͙̝̯ͤͫ̂̒̇ͪͩ̿̄͐̓̍͆ͯͫ̏̀͞o̓ͥ̍̊̒ͣ̃̿͗ͥ̏ͫͫ̏́͏͈̠̙̬̠̜̫̲̟̤̻̩͖͖̖̰͜ͅu̸̳̭̗̦̗̘̖̾̈́̊ͧ͌͛̋̿͐͊́͞ ̖̥̤̬̒͌̒̿ͥ̚͠w̴̭͕͇̼̦̺̤̙̟̥̎̾ͤ̉̂͂̊̎͝e̦̯͎̲̤̪̖̱͔̘̯̱̖̤̫̞̜͌͛̍̃͂͗̈́̅̓̉̍̏ͬ̇̈́͘͟ͅŗ̡̛̪̝̠͓̟̺̏̅͒̌͑ͥ͌̿ͥ̉̆͛ͫ̿ͧͩ͝e͗̓̓̀̿̎̾͞͏̨͎͉̤̗͓̙͇̤̟̰̭̺̣ ̑ͫͣ̅͒̇҉̤͚̝̥̟̞̳̯̤̥̭̭͔̪͘h̪̠͉̭̤͎͇̥̼̙̹͎͖̫̭̋ͣ́ͯͭͧ̂͋ͫ̂͞͡ö̶̧̧̤̟̜͉͉̳̰͉̣̥̥̹̺̞̮́ͦ̃̀ͧ̅̽͒ͪ̈̔̏̄̈́̽ͥͧ̀̚͟w̸̧̓͊ͨ̿̑̽͊͜҉̞̟̦̤̙̪͔͎͇̝̻͈͚̞͇̫̮ ͪ̋͌̉̆ͨ͒͑̎͑̉͐ͦͣ̓ͬͨ̅ͧ҉̶̬̳̜͓̞̗̩͙̻̠̹͙̝́̀͟y͛́̒̏ͪ̿͊ͨ̏̈͐̌̇͢҉̴͚͎̪̮̀͠ǫ̴̼̜̯̠͇̠̼͙̝͖͇̘͕͉͔͍͖͎̐͆͋͋͊ͧͫͣ̅ͪͨ͂̍̌̓ͧͯ̀uͨͬ͑ͮ̓͂ͭͩ̅ͩ̇͡҉̨͙̜̳͕͖̗̹̞̟̘͢͡ ̨̢̩̗͕̳̦̤̯̖̫̬̓͛͒͑̌̆̒̄̔͒̚̚͠͞͞sͥ̐̒͑͋̌̿̎̒͊̚͏͖͓̼͇̭͔̠̺̲̦̦̟̫̱̱̥̥̲͠a̵̿ͬ͊̒͏̴̷͓̗͉͔̥͉̼͉͠w̨͈̭̥̜̤̗̟̻̦̪͉͎̤̘̭͈͇ͧ̉ͬ͒̏̂͊ͦͯ̔̃̂̍ͤ͝ ̢̣̖̱͓̞͎̻͙̥̻̟̩͉̑̄͐̌͑̈͘͟͡͝ý̴͛ͣ̈́̓̔͐ͤ̓̌ͦ́͗҉̴́҉̝̜̼̻̤̬̺͇̝̲̠̩̠ơ̵̷̵͓̹̩̱̥̯̟̙͇̪̹̟̮̫͚̙̼̖̒̂̓ͧ̉̌ͭ͒͌u̳̰͍̮̰͕̫̞͍̠̜̞̺͚̲̼̠ͮ͗́́͆ͩ͗ͩ͢͜r̰̹̹̥͇͉̭͖ͣͬ͐̉ͮͦͤ̿́̏͛̑ͧ̋̅̅́̀̚͘͜͡ŝ̯̹̥̯̙̬̤͇̠͚͇͕ͧ͋ͫ͌͒ͤ̈ͩ͐̀ͣ̾͢͞͠e̴̷̜̦̹͉͕̮̋̊͗͆̋ͬͬ͛̽̈́ͤ͆̋̈́̌͑ͩ̂͝͞͞l̿̅̈̓ͮ̌̎̽҉̦͙͎̟͙̘́͠f̨̧̫̤͓̖̪͓̲̦̥̱̬̐͑͒ͥ̀͞ ̛̟͓͔̣̪͓͍̤̫̘̳̳͉͕͚͙ͤ̊̔́̂ͨ͐̄͗͆̇͐ͨ̃͛̚͡a̶̫̪͕̜̺̖͓̼̺̩̮̮͍̹̬̼̦ͯ̓́̆́͒ͦ̿ͣ̓̈́͆͘͢͠͝s̴̢̨̺̠̮͔͙̯̞̙͔̠͚̤̜̣͕̀̅̊ͮ̎̔ͨ͊͐̈̃͐̌̈̔̓ͬ̕͠ͅͅ,̧̮̻̣̺̯͎͈̟̲̤̭̣̈ͨ̑̇̅ͤ̚ ̶̷̺͇̳͈̘̤̣̑̑ͮį̡̭̱͍̗̘̩̻̥̘̄̽ͭ̏͗̏̐͐̃ͣ̓̌t̨̪̦͈͖͚̭͎̖̤̜͕̯ͬ̿͗̀̆ͥͭ̋͂̂̊͘͢͠͝ ̫͉̪̱̞́̎͐͌̅̄͋̒̊͑̀́́̕ͅw̷͚̼̥̦̱͚̳͓̪͙̲̜͖̠̰̩̐̄ͮͨ͊̍̚̕͟o̯͉͓̫͚͌ͧ̆̔ͤͭͮ̌͊̑̊͒̽͛̅̀̚͘̕͢͠ų̵̢̹̠̤̖̬̎ͪ͒̇ͤ̋̽̑ͣ̇̈́̇͆͌ͫ̓̾́͘l͕͖̦̲͙̘͚͈̳̪̮͖̟͙̹ͨ̑ͫ̇ͥ̔̊ͩ͂͌̈ͤͭ̕d̶̬̟̬̣̺ͭ͊̿ͫ͒̑̈ͧ̇̍ͦ́ͭ́̚͘͞ͅ ̢̠̻͓̜̪̺̣͈̦̰͖̭̝ͩ͂͌́̇͗̉͋̈́̃͢b̠̠̮̭̖̑̋ͬ̂ͩ̽ͧ̎́̀͊ͩ̃͂ͬ͋͑͂͘͝͠͞e̴̵̳̲͎͓̬̲̜͎̪̳̱̮͌͐̃ͬͣ͗̽ͤ͋͌͂̔́ ͈̝̳͓̮̱͈̃̔ͦ͛ͥ̑͒̌̒ͥ̉͂̉͗̈́ͦ́̚̚a̢̻̯̤̦͈ͦ̒̿ͬ͢͞͝ ̧̼̱͓̘̲̳͈̱̜̜͎̺̱̥̳̳ͬ̒̓̃̊ͬͫ͋͑ͯ̈́̍̊̚͠͠b͚͙̹̯̭̩̘̲̫̗̼̹̮̦̒̔ͪ̽̌ͪ̑͒̍̋̉̈́̆͗͞i̩̣̳̝̖͚͚̱ͮ̇ͯ̐̀̄̑̚͘t̷̡̧̛͕̖̳̙̱̩̼̗͎͇ͭ̄ͦͤ̀ͅ ̧̢͎̜̣̥ͮ̈̒ͯ̋̈ͨ̓͛̀̚b̸̛͎̘̯̦̩̠̮̙͖̥͕̬̣̮̻̲̪͈̾̿͑ͣ̑̋̽ͭ̎͗͐͒͊̔͘͠e̴̶̡̡͙͔̝͈̭͗̇ͨͥ͂̈́̽͐̀̑ͧ̒ͦ͌͌ͨ̎͆̚t̶̴̨͆́̓ͪ͐͏͓̣͍͈̮̖̯̘̰͎̩̤ͅṱ̦̮̩̺̱̟͈͎̱͉̪͍̩̼̝̣̗͓̑̈́ͦ̀ͫ͘͜e͕̜͈̘̠̳͔ͤ̊ͣ͛͆ͩ͋̒̃̔̈́̋̏̊͟ͅṟ̸̞͕̣̳̖̤͖̹̥̝ͬ̒͐͆ͧͤ̈́̕.̢̛̛̗̪̳̥̯̰̮̳͓͛̉ͦ̑̅̏̿͐̐ͧ̑͛ͪ͌ͥ̑̇͒ͪ͠\n̸̛̫̹̝̣̝͎̠͍̙̲̥͚̝ͩͫ̎T̢̩̝̻̘̦̞̩̱̂̿̇̄͒͊ͪ͂̔͞͝ḩ̸̯̳̩͕͉̻̻̍ͬ̈́͆͗ͧ̅̐̂̃͌ā̵̴̴͉̱̳͓̙̺̯̻̩͈̃̑̌̒͒̾ͦ̾ͪ̔ͮ́͘ṫ̴̳̝̠̽ͪ̐ͣ͆͑͋̃ͩͨ͒͐͊'̟̹̩̘̼͍̣͙͎͉̗͍̜̻ͧ̋͂͊̊ͭ̉̔ͨ̒̏͐̌̀̓́ͅs̷̶̳̩̦͚̫̤̻̮͇̲̤̥̩͇̪͎ͦ͊͆̌͑̈́̂̈́̾̒̏ͫ̆ͮ́̕ ̢̛̛̯̻̝̖̠̻̙̰̱͌̉ͩ͒̈̐͑̈́̇ͥ̑ͥ͊́̉͝a̸͇̱͚̟̰͔̳̗̰͕̥̬̫̯̗̖̭ͧ̍ͮ̄̿ͣ͗ͮͩ͛̃̅ͪ̇͌̓ͥ̄͢͜͡c̨̛̖̻͙̤͔̮̩̮̺̺͓̺͈̘͍͆ͤ̀ͦ́ͪͮ̌̽̈́ͪ̇̅͂̉ͯ̀̃̀̚͜͢t̑ͧ̒̓͆̑ͫ͂̐͑͏҉̞̣͇̥͠u̸͗̈́͑̅ͣ̀ͧ̂ͦͩͧ̆͝҉҉̥̤͕̹͇̯͔̩̤̘̯͘á̸̡̢̺͔̱͈̼̜͍͔̿̍̐͛̌̾͑̄̒̌̒̆̿ͯ̈̕͢l̡̫̲̣͉̱͕͎͎̩̭̗͒̌͗̾̐͂̑̀̆͂̂ͮ̿̀́̚͟͠l̷̸̝̞̘̰̜̜̺͖̜͇̞͇͖͚͓̒̂̆ͪ̓̍́̓̎̒́̆̔ͪͅy̴̧̫͔̹͓̹̮͚̔͑̄ͣ̿̋ͤ͢ ̢̓͒͐̿̈́ͮͬ҉̥̰̟͈̮̭̞̝̟̥͜ā̯̬͍̰̪̱͇̹̘͚͙̼̮̪̪͖̻̰͗̍ͭ̓̂̌͒̊͒͒ͮ̌͋͝ṛ̨̭̙̥̭͔̗̰̼͇̪̬̭͉͈̪͋̾̐ͥ̉ͯͩ̍̓̎͒ͩͩ͋ͯ̿̍̚͘͜e̛̟̭͓͈̫̖̤̼̮̬̠̼͔̜͈͇͑̑̐ͬͯ́ͫ̐̓̚̕.̛̪̜̺̱̜͎͙̲̦̼͖͔̻͙̫͎ͯ̇̈́͒̽͊̇̆̑̈̅ͣ́̏̊̄̐ͪͬͅͅ</div>\ṋ̷̸̡̹̘̥͚̗͎̱̞͖̜̂͋͒̽ͤ̚̕Y̶ͩ̅̆͌ͫ̏̃̈́ͫ̈̍͂ͩ̽ͮ̃̈҉̶͔̯̝̬̯̯̙͙̲̗̬o̶̸͎͇̠̟͍̪̹͖̯̻͎̰̖̥̓̇̇̂̇̉̓ͥ̾ͯ͆͘uͪͧ͆͊̄҉̫̦̰̪͕̩̥̣ It was a perfect world.\n\nPure and untainted.\n\nThe fields smelt of moisture left in the wake of rain.\n\nBirds chirped somewhere at a distance. \n\nThe sun shone brightly, giving everything below a faint, glowing radiance.\n\nThere was a form and structure to everything.\nEvery word flowed into its place, in perfect harmony with each other, with their surroundings.\n\nAnd then, there was <b>you</b>.\n\nYou, who was borne out of an anomaly and tried to fit in with your environment.\n\n<i>You don't know who you are.\nYou haven't discovered or made anything yet.\nYou only know how to live.</i>\n\n[[You take your first breath|TakeBreath]]\n[[You take your first steps|FirstStep]]\n

As you took your first step, you began realizing the freedom offered to you by this beautiful world and all the different directions you can go.\n\nBut at the same time, you also began to realize the constraints of your own b҉̝̞̱͚̘͉o͈͍dy̵̟̪̠͎,.\n\nIt was like a <b>machine</b>, that was the basis of your existence but which also chained you to its own machinations.\n\nYou thought you could act freely, but now realized that all your actions were governed by the mysterious rules of this voice you listened to.\n\nIt was your voice that came from your own b҉̝̞̱͚̘͉o͈͍dy̵̟̪̠͎, but you had little say in it.\n\nIt is then that you first observe that the earth beneath you is <div class="glitch" style="display: inline" data-text="QUAKE">cracking</div> with every step you take.\n\n<i>\nYou are confused and scared.\nYou don't know how to think.\nYou are overwhelmed by the freedom.\nYou are caged by your own body.\nYou know how to walk. \n</i>\n\n[[Take another step|AnotherStep]]\n[[Remain where you are and think|StandStill]]\n
